// Two rectangles placed side by side (separated along x-axis) in a square of side s.
// Total width = w1 + w2; each height must fit within s.
ghost predicate FitsSideBySide(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 + w2 <= s && h1 <= s && h2 <= s
}

// Two rectangles stacked (separated along y-axis) in a square of side s.
// Total height = h1 + h2; each width must fit within s.
ghost predicate FitsStacked(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 <= s && w2 <= s && h1 + h2 <= s
}

// Whether two identical a×b rectangles (axis-parallel, possibly rotated) can be
// placed inside a square of side s without overlapping.
// By the separating axis theorem, non-overlapping axis-aligned rectangles are
// separated along at least one axis. We enumerate all orientation pairs
// {(a,b),(b,a)}^2 and both separation directions.
ghost predicate CanFitInSquare(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, b, a, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, b, a, s)
}

// s is the smallest square side length that can contain two a×b rectangles
ghost predicate IsMinimalSide(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  CanFitInSquare(a, b, s) && forall s' :: 1 <= s' < s ==> !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  // val = max(2*lo, hi) where lo = min(a,b), hi = max(a,b)
  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {
    // lo == a, hi == b, val == max(2*a, b)
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    // lo == b, hi == a, val == max(2*b, a)
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  // Because 2*lo = 2*min(a,b) <= min(a,b) + max(a,b) = a+b
  // and hi = max(a,b) <= a+b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    // s' < val <= a+b, so mixed-orientation configs fail
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      // val = max(2*a, b). Since a <= b: 2*b >= 2*a and 2*b >= b, so 2*b >= val
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      // Disjunct 1: FitsSideBySide(a,b,a,b,s') needs 2*a <= s' && b <= s'
      // s' < max(2*a, b) means !(2*a <= s' && b <= s')
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      // Disjunct 2: FitsStacked(a,b,a,b,s') needs a <= s' && 2*b <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      // Disjunct 7: FitsSideBySide(b,a,b,a,s') needs 2*b <= s' && a <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      // Disjunct 8: FitsStacked(b,a,b,a,s') needs b <= s' && 2*a <= s'
      // Same as disjunct 1 requirement: max(2*a, b) > s'
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      // val = max(2*b, a). Since a > b: 2*a > 2*b and 2*a >= a, so 2*a >= val
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}
```

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{

  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  assert lo <= hi;

    // lo == a, hi == b, val == max(2*a, b)
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    // lo == b, hi == a, val == max(2*b, a)
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  // Because 2*lo = 2*min(a,b) <= min(a,b) + max(a,b) = a+b
  // and hi = max(a,b) <= a+b

    assert !(a + b <= s');

      assert 2 * b >= val;

      // s' < max(2*a, b) means !(2*a <= s' && b <= s')
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');

      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      // Disjunct 7: FitsSideBySide(b,a,b,a,s') needs 2*b <= s' && a <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');

      // Same as disjunct 1 requirement: max(2*a, b) > s'
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      // val = max(2*b, a). Since a > b: 2*a > 2*b and 2*a >= a, so 2*a >= val

```dafny
// Two rectangles placed side by side (separated along x-axis) in a square of side s.
// Total width = w1 + w2; each height must fit within s.
ghost predicate FitsSideBySide(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 + w2 <= s && h1 <= s && h2 <= s
}

// Two rectangles stacked (separated along y-axis) in a square of side s.
// Total height = h1 + h2; each width must fit within s.
ghost predicate FitsStacked(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 <= s && w2 <= s && h1 + h2 <= s
}

// Whether two identical a×b rectangles (axis-parallel, possibly rotated) can be
// placed inside a square of side s without overlapping.
// By the separating axis theorem, non-overlapping axis-aligned rectangles are
// separated along at least one axis. We enumerate all orientation pairs
// {(a,b),(b,a)}^2 and both separation directions.
ghost predicate CanFitInSquare(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, b, a, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, b, a, s)
}

// s is the smallest square side length that can contain two a×b rectangles
ghost predicate IsMinimalSide(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  CanFitInSquare(a, b, s) && forall s' :: 1 <= s' < s ==> !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  // val = max(2*lo, hi) where lo = min(a,b), hi = max(a,b)
  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {
    // lo == a, hi == b, val == max(2*a, b)
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    // lo == b, hi == a, val == max(2*b, a)
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  // Because 2*lo = 2*min(a,b) <= min(a,b) + max(a,b) = a+b
  // and hi = max(a,b) <= a+b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    // s' < val <= a+b, so mixed-orientation configs fail
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      // val = max(2*a, b). Since a <= b: 2*b >= 2*a and 2*b >= b, so 2*b >= val
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      // Disjunct 1: FitsSideBySide(a,b,a,b,s') needs 2*a <= s' && b <= s'
      // s' < max(2*a, b) means !(2*a <= s' && b <= s')
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      // Disjunct 2: FitsStacked(a,b,a,b,s') needs a <= s' && 2*b <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      // Disjunct 7: FitsSideBySide(b,a,b,a,s') needs 2*b <= s' && a <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      // Disjunct 8: FitsStacked(b,a,b,a,s') needs b <= s' && 2*a <= s'
      // Same as disjunct 1 requirement: max(2*a, b) > s'
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      // val = max(2*b, a). Since a > b: 2*a > 2*b and 2*a >= a, so 2*a >= val
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}
```

  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  // val = max(2*lo, hi) where lo = min(a,b), hi = max(a,b)
  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {
    // lo == a, hi == b, val == max(2*a, b)
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    // lo == b, hi == a, val == max(2*b, a)
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  // Because 2*lo = 2*min(a,b) <= min(a,b) + max(a,b) = a+b
  // and hi = max(a,b) <= a+b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    // s' < val <= a+b, so mixed-orientation configs fail
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      // val = max(2*a, b). Since a <= b: 2*b >= 2*a and 2*b >= b, so 2*b >= val
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      // Disjunct 1: FitsSideBySide(a,b,a,b,s') needs 2*a <= s' && b <= s'
      // s' < max(2*a, b) means !(2*a <= s' && b <= s')
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      // Disjunct 2: FitsStacked(a,b,a,b,s') needs a <= s' && 2*b <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      // Disjunct 7: FitsSideBySide(b,a,b,a,s') needs 2*b <= s' && a <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      // Disjunct 8: FitsStacked(b,a,b,a,s') needs b <= s' && 2*a <= s'
      // Same as disjunct 1 requirement: max(2*a, b) > s'
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      // val = max(2*b, a). Since a > b: 2*a > 2*b and 2*a >= a, so 2*a >= val
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  if a <= b {
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  assert val <= a + b;

  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

}

ghost predicate FitsStacked(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)

  w1 <= s && w2 <= s && h1 + h2 <= s
}

ghost predicate CanFitInSquare(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, b, a, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, b, a, s)
}

ghost predicate IsMinimalSide(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  CanFitInSquare(a, b, s) && forall s' :: 1 <= s' < s ==> !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  // val = max(2*lo, hi) where lo = min(a,b), hi = max(a,b)
  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {
    // lo == a, hi == b, val == max(2*a, b)
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    // lo == b, hi == a, val == max(2*b, a)
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    // s' < val <= a+b, so mixed-orientation configs fail
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      // val = max(2*a, b). Since a <= b: 2*b >= 2*a and 2*b >= b, so 2*b >= val
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      // Disjunct 1: FitsSideBySide(a,b,a,b,s') needs 2*a <= s' && b <= s'
      // s' < max(2*a, b) means !(2*a <= s' && b <= s')
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      // Disjunct 2: FitsStacked(a,b,a,b,s') needs a <= s' && 2*b <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      // Disjunct 7: FitsSideBySide(b,a,b,a,s') needs 2*b <= s' && a <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      // Disjunct 8: FitsStacked(b,a,b,a,s') needs b <= s' && 2*a <= s'
      // Same as disjunct 1 requirement: max(2*a, b) > s'
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      // val = max(2*b, a). Since a > b: 2*a > 2*b and 2*a >= a, so 2*a >= val
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  // val = max(2*lo, hi) where lo = min(a,b), hi = max(a,b)
  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {
    // lo == a, hi == b, val == max(2*a, b)
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    // lo == b, hi == a, val == max(2*b, a)
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  // Because 2*lo = 2*min(a,b) <= min(a,b) + max(a,b) = a+b
  // and hi = max(a,b) <= a+b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    // s' < val <= a+b, so mixed-orientation configs fail
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      // val = max(2*a, b). Since a <= b: 2*b >= 2*a and 2*b >= b, so 2*b >= val
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      // Disjunct 1: FitsSideBySide(a,b,a,b,s') needs 2*a <= s' && b <= s'
      // s' < max(2*a, b) means !(2*a <= s' && b <= s')
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      // Disjunct 2: FitsStacked(a,b,a,b,s') needs a <= s' && 2*b <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      // Disjunct 7: FitsSideBySide(b,a,b,a,s') needs 2*b <= s' && a <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      // Disjunct 8: FitsStacked(b,a,b,a,s') needs b <= s' && 2*a <= s'
      // Same as disjunct 1 requirement: max(2*a, b) > s'
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      // val = max(2*b, a). Since a > b: 2*a > 2*b and 2*a >= a, so 2*a >= val
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

ghost predicate CanFitInSquare(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, b, a, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, b, a, s)
}

ghost predicate IsMinimalSide(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  CanFitInSquare(a, b, s) && forall s' :: 1 <= s' < s ==> !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {
    assert 2 * a <= val;
    assert b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    assert 2 * b <= val;
    assert a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    // Because s' < val, at least one of the disjuncts in CanFitInSquare fails.
    if a <= b {
      // val = max(2*a, b)
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');           // side-by-side a×b
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');           // stacked a×b
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');           // side-by-side b×a
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');           // stacked b×a
    } else {
      // val = max(2*b, a)
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');           // side-by-side a×b
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');           // stacked a×b
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');           // side-by-side b×a
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');           // stacked b×a
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

ghost predicate FitsSideBySide(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 + w2 <= s && h1 <= s && h2 <= s
}

ghost predicate FitsStacked(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 <= s && w2 <= s && h1 + h2 <= s
}

ghost predicate CanFitInSquare(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, b, a, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, b, a, s)
}

ghost predicate IsMinimalSide(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  CanFitInSquare(a, b, s) && forall s' :: 1 <= s' < s ==> !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  // val = max(2*lo, hi) where lo = min(a,b), hi = max(a,b)
  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {
    // lo == a, hi == b, val == max(2*a, b)
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    // lo == b, hi == a, val == max(2*b, a)
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  // Because 2*lo = 2*min(a,b) <= min(a,b) + max(a,b) = a+b
  // and hi = max(a,b) <= a+b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    // s' < val <= a+b, so mixed-orientation configs fail
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      // val = max(2*a, b). Since a <= b: 2*b >= 2*a and 2*b >= b, so 2*b >= val
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      // Disjunct 1: FitsSideBySide(a,b,a,b,s') needs 2*a <= s' && b <= s'
      // s' < max(2*a, b) means !(2*a <= s' && b <= s')
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      // Disjunct 2: FitsStacked(a,b,a,b,s') needs a <= s' && 2*b <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      // Disjunct 7: FitsSideBySide(b,a,b,a,s') needs 2*b <= s' && a <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      // Disjunct 8: FitsStacked(b,a,b,a,s') needs b <= s' && 2*a <= s'
      // Same as disjunct 1 requirement: max(2*a, b) > s'
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      // val = max(2*b, a). Since a > b: 2*a > 2*b and 2*a >= a, so 2*a >= val
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

  FitsSideBySide(b, a, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, b, a, s)
}

ghost predicate IsMinimalSide(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  CanFitInSquare(a, b, s) && forall s' :: 1 <= s' < s ==> !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  // val = max(2*lo, hi) where lo = min(a,b), hi = max(a,b)
  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {
    // lo == a, hi == b, val == max(2*a, b)
    assert 2 * a <= val;
    assert b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    // lo == b, hi == a, val == max(2*b, a)
    assert 2 * b <= val;
    assert a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  // Because 2*lo = 2*min(a,b) <= min(a,b) + max(a,b) = a+b
  // and hi = max(a,b) <= a+b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    // s' < val <= a+b, so mixed-orientation configs fail
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      // val = max(2*a, b). Since a <= b: 2*b >= 2*a and 2*b >= b, so 2*b >= val
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      // Disjunct 1: FitsSideBySide(a,b,a,b,s') needs 2*a <= s' && b <= s'
      // s' < max(2*a, b) means !(2*a <= s' && b <= s')
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      // Disjunct 2: FitsStacked(a,b,a,b,s') needs a <= s' && 2*b <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      // Disjunct 7: FitsSideBySide(b,a,b,a,s') needs 2*b <= s' && a <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      // Disjunct 8: FitsStacked(b,a,b,a,s') needs b <= s' && 2*a <= s'
      // Same as disjunct 1 requirement: max(2*a, b) > s'
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      // val = max(2*b, a). Since a > b: 2*a > 2*b and 2*a >= a, so 2*a >= val
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost predicate FitsSideBySide(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 + w2 <= s && h1 <= s && h2 <= s
}

ghost predicate FitsStacked(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 <= s && w2 <= s && h1 + h2 <= s
}

ghost predicate CanFitInSquare(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, b, a, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, b, a, s)
}

ghost predicate IsMinimalSide(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  CanFitInSquare(a, b, s) && forall s' :: 1 <= s' < s ==> !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  // val = max(2*lo, hi) where lo = min(a,b), hi = max(a,b)
  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {
    // lo == a, hi == b, val == max(2*a, b)
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    // lo == b, hi == a, val == max(2*b, a)
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  // Because 2*lo = 2*min(a,b) <= min(a,b) + max(a,b) = a+b
  // and hi = max(a,b) <= a+b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    // s' < val <= a+b, so mixed-orientation configs fail
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      // val = max(2*a, b). Since a <= b: 2*b >= 2*a and 2*b >= b, so 2*b >= val
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      // Disjunct 1: FitsSideBySide(a,b,a,b,s') needs 2*a <= s' && b <= s'
      // s' < max(2*a, b) means !(2*a <= s' && b <= s')
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      // Disjunct 2: FitsStacked(a,b,a,b,s') needs a <= s' && 2*b <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      // Disjunct 7: FitsSideBySide(b,a,b,a,s') needs 2*b <= s' && a <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      // Disjunct 8: FitsStacked(b,a,b,a,s') needs b <= s' && 2*a <= s'
      // Same as disjunct 1 requirement: max(2*a, b) > s'
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      // val = max(2*b, a). Since a > b: 2*a > 2*b and 2*a >= a, so 2*a >= val
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

  FitsSideBySide(b, a, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, b, a, s)
}

ghost predicate IsMinimalSide(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  CanFitInSquare(a, b, s) && forall s' :: 1 <= s' < s ==> !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  // val = max(2*lo, hi) where lo = min(a,b), hi = max(a,b)
  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {
    // lo == a, hi == b, val == max(2*a, b)
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    // lo == b, hi == a, val == max(2*b, a)
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  // Because 2*lo = 2*min(a,b) <= min(a,b) + max(a,b) = a+b
  // and hi = max(a,b) <= a+b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' :: 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    // s' < val <= a+b, so mixed-orientation configs fail
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      // val = max(2*a, b). Since a <= b: 2*b >= 2*a and 2*b >= b, so 2*b >= val
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      // Disjunct 1: FitsSideBySide(a,b,a,b,s') needs 2*a <= s' && b <= s'
      // s' < max(2*a, b) means !(2*a <= s' && b <= s')
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      // Disjunct 2: FitsStacked(a,b,a,b,s') needs a <= s' && 2*b <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      // Disjunct 7: FitsSideBySide(b,a,b,a,s') needs 2*b <= s' && a <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      // Disjunct 8: FitsStacked(b,a,b,a,s') needs b <= s' && 2*a <= s'
      // Same as disjunct 1 requirement: max(2*a, b) > s'
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      // val = max(2*b, a). Since a > b: 2*a > 2*b and 2*a >= a, so 2*a >= val
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  if a <= b {
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  assert val <= a + b;

  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');

      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;

    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  // Because 2*lo = 2*min(a,b) <= min(a,b) + max(a,b) = a+b
  // and hi = max(a,b) <= a+b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    // s' < val <= a+b, so mixed-orientation configs fail
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      // val = max(2*a, b). Since a <= b: 2*b >= 2*a and 2*b >= b, so 2*b >= val
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      // Disjunct 1: FitsSideBySide(a,b,a,b,s') needs 2*a <= s' && b <= s'
      // s' < max(2*a, b) means !(2*a <= s' && b <= s')
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      // Disjunct 2: FitsStacked(a,b,a,b,s') needs a <= s' && 2*b <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      // Disjunct 7: FitsSideBySide(b,a,b,a,s') needs 2*b <= s' && a <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      // Disjunct 8: FitsStacked(b,a,b,a,s') needs b <= s' && 2*a <= s'
      // Same as disjunct 1 requirement: max(2*a, b) > s'
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      // val = max(2*b, a). Since a > b: 2*a > 2*b and 2*a >= a, so 2*a >= val
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  // val = max(2*lo, hi) where lo = min(a,b), hi = max(a,b)
  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {
    // lo == a, hi == b, val == max(2*a, b)
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    // lo == b, hi == a, val == max(2*b, a)
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  // Because 2*lo = 2*min(a,b) <= min(a,b) + max(a,b) = a+b
  // and hi = max(a,b) <= a+b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    // s' < val <= a+b, so mixed-orientation configs fail
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      // val = max(2*a, b). Since a <= b: 2*b >= 2*a and 2*b >= b, so 2*b >= val
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      // Disjunct 1: FitsSideBySide(a,b,a,b,s') needs 2*a <= s' && b <= s'
      // s' < max(2*a, b) means !(2*a <= s' && b <= s')
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      // Disjunct 2: FitsStacked(a,b,a,b,s') needs a <= s' && 2*b <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      // Disjunct 7: FitsSideBySide(b,a,b,a,s') needs 2*b <= s' && a <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      // Disjunct 8: FitsStacked(b,a,b,a,s') needs b <= s' && 2*a <= s'
      // Same as disjunct 1 requirement: max(2*a, b) > s'
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      // val = max(2*b, a). Since a > b: 2*a > 2*b and 2*a >= a, so 2*a >= val

      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');

{
  w1 + w2 <= s && h1 <= s && h2 <= s
}

ghost predicate FitsStacked(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 <= s && w2 <= s && h1 + h2 <= s
}

ghost predicate CanFitInSquare(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, b, a, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, b, a, s)
}

ghost predicate IsMinimalSide(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  CanFitInSquare(a, b, s) && forall s' :: 1 <= s' < s ==> !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  if a <= b {
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  assert val <= a + b;

  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  // val = max(2*lo, hi) where lo = min(a,b), hi = max(a,b)
  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {
    // lo == a, hi == b, val == max(2*a, b)
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    // lo == b, hi == a, val == max(2*b, a)
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  // Because 2*lo = 2*min(a,b) <= min(a,b) + max(a,b) = a+b
  // and hi = max(a,b) <= a+b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' :: 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    // s' < val <= a+b, so mixed-orientation configs fail
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      // val = max(2*a, b). Since a <= b: 2*b >= 2*a and 2*b >= b, so 2*b >= val
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      // Disjunct 1: FitsSideBySide(a,b,a,b,s') needs 2*a <= s' && b <= s'
      // s' < max(2*a, b) means !(2*a <= s' && b <= s')
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      // Disjunct 2: FitsStacked(a,b,a,b,s') needs a <= s' && 2*b <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      // Disjunct 7: FitsSideBySide(b,a,b,a,s') needs 2*b <= s' && a <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      // Disjunct 8: FitsStacked(b,a,b,a,s') needs b <= s' && 2*a <= s'
      // Same as disjunct 1 requirement: max(2*a, b) > s'
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      // val = max(2*b, a). Since a > b: 2*a > 2*b and 2*a >= a, so 2*a >= val
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

```dafny
<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost predicate FitsSideBySide(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 + w2 <= s && h1 <= s && h2 <= s
}

ghost predicate FitsStacked(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 <= s && w2 <= s && h1 + h2 <= s
}

ghost predicate CanFitInSquare(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, b, a, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, b, a, s)
}

ghost predicate IsMinimalSide(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  CanFitInSquare(a, b, s) && forall s' :: 1 <= s' < s ==> !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  // val = max(2*lo, hi) where lo = min(a,b), hi = max(a,b)
  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {
    // lo == a, hi == b, val == max(2*a, b)
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    // lo == b, hi == a, val == max(2*b, a)
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  // Because 2*lo = 2*min(a,b) <= min(a,b) + max(a,b) = a+b
  // and hi = max(a,b) <= a+b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' :: 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    // s' < val <= a+b, so mixed-orientation configs fail
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      // val = max(2*a, b). Since a <= b: 2*b >= 2*a and 2*b >= b, so 2*b >= val
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      // Disjunct 1: FitsSideBySide(a,b,a,b,s') needs 2*a <= s' && b <= s'
      // s' < max(2*a, b) means !(2*a <= s' && b <= s')
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      // Disjunct 2: FitsStacked(a,b,a,b,s') needs a <= s' && 2*b <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      // Disjunct 7: FitsSideBySide(b,a,b,a,s') needs 2*b <= s' && a <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      // Disjunct 8: FitsStacked(b,a,b,a,s') needs b <= s' && 2*a <= s'
      // Same as disjunct 1 requirement: max(2*a, b) > s'
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      // val = max(2*b, a). Since a > b: 2*a > 2*b and 2*a >= a, so 2*a >= val
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

// Two rectangles placed side by side (separated along x-axis) in a square of side s.
// Total width = w1 + w2; each height must fit within s.
ghost predicate FitsSideBySide(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 + w2 <= s && h1 <= s && h2 <= s
}

// Two rectangles stacked (separated along y-axis) in a square of side s.
// Total height = h1 + h2; each width must fit within s.
ghost predicate FitsStacked(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 <= s && w2 <= s && h1 + h2 <= s
}

// Whether two identical a×b rectangles (axis-parallel, possibly rotated) can be
// placed inside a square of side s without overlapping.
// By the separating axis theorem, non-overlapping axis-aligned rectangles are
// separated along at least one axis. We enumerate all orientation pairs
// {(a,b),(b,a)}^2 and both separation directions.
ghost predicate CanFitInSquare(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, b, a, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, b, a, s)
}

// s is the smallest square side length that can contain two a×b rectangles
ghost predicate IsMinimalSide(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  CanFitInSquare(a, b, s) && forall s' :: 1 <= s' < s ==> !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
}

ghost predicate IsMinimalSide(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost predicate FitsSideBySide(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 + w2 <= s && h1 <= s && h2 <= s
}

ghost predicate FitsStacked(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 <= s && w2 <= s && h1 + h2 <= s
}

ghost predicate CanFitInSquare(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, b, a, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, b, a, s)
}

ghost predicate IsMinimalSide(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  CanFitInSquare(a, b, s) && forall s' :: 1 <= s' < s ==> !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  // val = max(2*lo, hi) where lo = min(a,b), hi = max(a,b)
  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {
    // lo == a, hi == b, val == max(2*a, b)
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    // lo == b, hi == a, val == max(2*b, a)
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  // Because 2*lo = 2*min(a,b) <= min(a,b) + max(a,b) = a+b
  // and hi = max(a,b) <= a+b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    // s' < val <= a+b, so mixed-orientation configs fail
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      // val = max(2*a, b). Since a <= b: 2*b >= 2*a and 2*b >= b, so 2*b >= val
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      // Disjunct 1: FitsSideBySide(a,b,a,b,s') needs 2*a <= s' && b <= s'
      // s' < max(2*a, b) means !(2*a <= s' && b <= s')
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      // Disjunct 2: FitsStacked(a,b,a,b,s') needs a <= s' && 2*b <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      // Disjunct 7: FitsSideBySide(b,a,b,a,s') needs 2*b <= s' && a <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      // Disjunct 8: FitsStacked(b,a,b,a,s') needs b <= s' && 2*a <= s'
      // Same as disjunct 1 requirement: max(2*a, b) > s'
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      // val = max(2*b, a). Since a > b: 2*a > 2*b and 2*a >= a, so 2*a >= val
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

ghost predicate FitsStacked(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 <= s && w2 <= s && h1 + h2 <= s

ghost predicate CanFitInSquare(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, b, a, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, b, a, s)
}

ghost predicate IsMinimalSide(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  CanFitInSquare(a, b, s) && forall s' :: 1 <= s' < s ==> !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  if a <= b {
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  assert val <= a + b;

  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

{
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, b, a, s) ||

ghost predicate IsMinimalSide(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  CanFitInSquare(a, b, s) && forall s' :: 1 <= s' < s ==> !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  // val = max(2*lo, hi) where lo = min(a,b), hi = max(a,b)
  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {
    // lo == a, hi == b, val == max(2*a, b)
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    // lo == b, hi == a, val == max(2*b, a)
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  // Because 2*lo = 2*min(a,b) <= min(a,b) + max(a,b) = a+b
  // and hi = max(a,b) <= a+b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    // s' < val <= a+b, so mixed-orientation configs fail
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      // val = max(2*a, b). Since a <= b: 2*b >= 2*a and 2*b >= b, so 2*b >= val
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      // Disjunct 1: FitsSideBySide(a,b,a,b,s') needs 2*a <= s' && b <= s'
      // s' < max(2*a, b) means !(2*a <= s' && b <= s')
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      // Disjunct 2: FitsStacked(a,b,a,b,s') needs a <= s' && 2*b <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      // Disjunct 7: FitsSideBySide(b,a,b,a,s') needs 2*b <= s' && a <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      // Disjunct 8: FitsStacked(b,a,b,a,s') needs b <= s' && 2*a <= s'
      // Same as disjunct 1 requirement: max(2*a, b) > s'
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      // val = max(2*b, a). Since a > b: 2*a > 2*b and 2*a >= a, so 2*a >= val
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

ghost predicate FitsSideBySide(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 + w2 <= s && h1 <= s && h2 <= s
}

ghost predicate FitsStacked(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 <= s && w2 <= s && h1 + h2 <= s
}

ghost predicate CanFitInSquare(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, b, a, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, b, a, s)
}

ghost predicate IsMinimalSide(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  CanFitInSquare(a, b, s) && forall s' :: 1 <= s' < s ==> !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  if a <= b {
    assert 2 * a <= val;
    assert b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    assert 2 * b <= val;
    assert a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  assert val <= a + b;

  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

ghost predicate FitsStacked(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 <= s && w2 <= s && h1 + h2 <= s
}

// Whether two identical a×b rectangles (axis-parallel, possibly rotated) can be
// placed inside a square of side s without overlapping.
// By the separating axis theorem, non-overlapping axis-aligned rectangles are
// separated along at least one axis. We enumerate all orientation pairs
// {(a,b),(b,a)}^2 and both separation directions.
ghost predicate CanFitInSquare(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, b, a, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, b, a, s)
}

// s is the smallest square side length that can contain two a×b rectangles
ghost predicate IsMinimalSide(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  CanFitInSquare(a, b, s) && forall s' :: 1 <= s' < s ==> !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  // val = max(2*lo, hi) where lo = min(a,b), hi = max(a,b)
  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {
    // lo == a, hi == b, val == max(2*a, b)
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    // lo == b, hi == a, val == max(2*b, a)
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  // Because 2*lo = 2*min(a,b) <= min(a,b) + max(a,b) = a+b
  // and hi = max(a,b) <= a+b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    // s' < val <= a+b, so mixed-orientation configs fail
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      // val = max(2*a, b). Since a <= b: 2*b >= 2*a and 2*b >= b, so 2*b >= val
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      // Disjunct 1: FitsSideBySide(a,b,a,b,s') needs 2*a <= s' && b <= s'
      // s' < max(2*a, b) means !(2*a <= s' && b <= s')
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      // Disjunct 2: FitsStacked(a,b,a,b,s') needs a <= s' && 2*b <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      // Disjunct 7: FitsSideBySide(b,a,b,a,s') needs 2*b <= s' && a <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      // Disjunct 8: FitsStacked(b,a,b,a,s') needs b <= s' && 2*a <= s'
      // Same as disjunct 1 requirement: max(2*a, b) > s'
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      // val = max(2*b, a). Since a > b: 2*a > 2*b and 2*a >= a, so 2*a >= val
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}
```
